## תָּא (id: 007685000000000)

תָּא
====

תָּא (H8372)

noun m

Buildings

room, recess, alcove \= a part of a building enclosed by three walls only

[1KI 14:28](https://ref.ly/1Kgs14:28) · [2CH 12:11](https://ref.ly/2Chr12:11) · [EZK 40:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:7) · [EZK 40:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:7) · [EZK 40:10](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:10) · [EZK 40:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:12) · [EZK 40:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:12) · [EZK 40:13](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:13) · [EZK 40:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:16) · [EZK 40:21](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:21) · [EZK 40:29](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:29) · [EZK 40:33](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:33) · [EZK 40:36](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:36)

1 EZK 40:21 · EZK 40:29 · EZK 40:33 · EZK 40:36 MT\-K תאו \| MT\-Q תָאָיו

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** 1 Kings 14:28; 2 Chronicles 12:11; Ezekiel 40:7; Ezekiel 40:10; Ezekiel 40:12; Ezekiel 40:13; Ezekiel 40:16; Ezekiel 40:21; Ezekiel 40:29; Ezekiel 40:33; Ezekiel 40:36

תאב

verb · תַּאֲבָה

Wish 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to long, to desire \= process by which someone experiences a desire to know or do something, or for something to happen; ≈ only used in connection with God

[PSA 119:40](https://ref.ly/Ps119:40) · [PSA 119:174](https://ref.ly/Ps119:174)

verb

Hate 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ שׂנא

to hate, to abhor, to detest \= state in which someone experiences a deep loathing for something

Reinier de Blois

## תְּאֹו (id: 007689000000000)

תְּאֹו
======

תְּאֹו (H8377)

noun m

Wild Animals

oryx \= medium\-sized antelope, about the size of a donkey, with long slender horns that are usually over a meter long; these horns are almost straight and slope back from the animal’s head at about thirty degrees from the perpendicular; the adults are a light fawn color with dark brown markings on the face and on the lower part of both front and back legs; the belly is white; ◄ Oryx leucoryx; ► unclean and therefore not to be eaten

[DEU 14:5](https://ref.ly/Deut14:5) · [ISA 51:20](https://ref.ly/Isa51:20)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 14:5; Isaiah 51:20


## תַּאֲוָה (id: 007690000000000)

תַּאֲוָה
========

תַּאֲוָה (H8378 · H8379)

noun f · אוה · קִבְרֹות הַתַּאֲוָה

Hunger

craving, desire \= process by which someone senses a physical craving for food

[NUM 11:4](https://ref.ly/Num11:4) · [PSA 78:29](https://ref.ly/Ps78:29) · [PSA 78:30](https://ref.ly/Ps78:30) · [PSA 106:14](https://ref.ly/Ps106:14)

Wish 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ אֲנָחָה · אֲרֶשֶׁת · תֹּוחֶלֶת · תִּקְוָה 

|  |
| --- |

 ≠ מְגֹורָה

desire, longing \= state in which humans experience a desire to see something happen or do something oneself; ◄ this desire is associated with one's heart or throat ≈ and can be both good and evil

[PSA 10:3](https://ref.ly/Ps10:3) · [PSA 10:17](https://ref.ly/Ps10:17) · [PSA 21:3](https://ref.ly/Ps21:3) · [PSA 38:10](https://ref.ly/Ps38:10) · [PSA 112:10](https://ref.ly/Ps112:10) · [PRO 10:24](https://ref.ly/Prov10:24) · [PRO 11:23](https://ref.ly/Prov11:23) · [PRO 13:12](https://ref.ly/Prov13:12) · [PRO 13:19](https://ref.ly/Prov13:19) · [PRO 18:1](https://ref.ly/Prov18:1) · [PRO 19:22](https://ref.ly/Prov19:22) · [PRO 21:25](https://ref.ly/Prov21:25) · [PRO 21:26](https://ref.ly/Prov21:26) · [ISA 26:8](https://ref.ly/Isa26:8)

Wish 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ בְּרָכָה

choice, delight, bounty \= something desirable

[GEN 3:6](https://ref.ly/Gen3:6) · [GEN 49:26](https://ref.ly/Gen49:26) · [JOB 33:20](https://ref.ly/Job33:20)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 11:4; Psalms 78:29; Psalms 78:30; Psalms 106:14; Psalms 10:3; Psalms 10:17; Psalms 21:3; Psalms 38:10; Psalms 112:10; Proverbs 10:24; Proverbs 11:23; Proverbs 13:12; Proverbs 13:19; Proverbs 18:1; Proverbs 19:22; Proverbs 21:25; Proverbs 21:26; Isaiah 26:8; Genesis 3:6; Genesis 49:26; Job 33:20


## תַּאֲלָה (id: 007691000000000)

תַּאֲלָה
========

תַּאֲלָה (H8381) — תַּאְלָה

noun f · אלה

Curse

curse \= action by which someone invokes the name of a deity and ask him to punish a wrong\-doer; ◄ contexts in which this may happen include: (1\) covenants and agreements, where the deity is asked to punish those who do not obey the terms of the agreement, (2\) cases where a supposedly wrongful act has been committed, but where there is not enough certainty about the identity of the person who is responsible, and (3\) in order to prevent people from committing a wrongful action, knowing that the deity's punishment will be upon them if they do so; ► the effectiveness of the curse partially depends on the authority of the one pronouncing it

[LAM 3:65](https://ref.ly/Lam3:65)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Lamentations 3:65

## תְּאֵנָה (id: 007693000000000)

תְּאֵנָה
========

תְּאֵנָה (H8384)

noun f

Trees 

|  |
| --- |

 Fruits 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ גֶּפֶן

fig tree, fig \= a tree that reaches a height of 5–8 m, with a round crown and very deep roots; its fruit is about the size of a hen’s egg and can be green, yellow, purple, or brown depending on the type; ◄ Ficus carica; ► the fruits are sweet and soft; ≈ the image of peace and happiness in Israel was: “every man under his vine and under his fig tree"

[GEN 3:7](https://ref.ly/Gen3:7) · [NUM 13:23](https://ref.ly/Num13:23) · [NUM 20:5](https://ref.ly/Num20:5) · [DEU 8:8](https://ref.ly/Deut8:8) · [JDG 9:10](https://ref.ly/Judg9:10) · [JDG 9:11](https://ref.ly/Judg9:11) · [1KI 5:5](https://ref.ly/1Kgs5:5) · [2KI 18:31](https://ref.ly/2Kgs18:31) · [2KI 20:7](https://ref.ly/2Kgs20:7) · [NEH 13:15](https://ref.ly/Neh13:15) · [PSA 105:33](https://ref.ly/Ps105:33) · [PRO 27:18](https://ref.ly/Prov27:18) · [SNG 2:13](https://ref.ly/Song2:13) · [ISA 34:4](https://ref.ly/Isa34:4) · [ISA 36:16](https://ref.ly/Isa36:16) · [ISA 38:21](https://ref.ly/Isa38:21) · [JER 5:17](https://ref.ly/Jer5:17) · [JER 8:13](https://ref.ly/Jer8:13) · [JER 8:13](https://ref.ly/Jer8:13) · [JER 24:1](https://ref.ly/Jer24:1) · [JER 24:2](https://ref.ly/Jer24:2) · [JER 24:2](https://ref.ly/Jer24:2) · [JER 24:2](https://ref.ly/Jer24:2) · [JER 24:3](https://ref.ly/Jer24:3) · [JER 24:3](https://ref.ly/Jer24:3) · [JER 24:5](https://ref.ly/Jer24:5) · [JER 24:8](https://ref.ly/Jer24:8) · [JER 29:17](https://ref.ly/Jer29:17) · [HOS 2:14](https://ref.ly/Hos2:14) · [HOS 9:10](https://ref.ly/Hos9:10) · [JOL 1:7](https://ref.ly/Joel1:7) · [JOL 1:12](https://ref.ly/Joel1:12) · [JOL 2:22](https://ref.ly/Joel2:22) · [AMO 4:9](https://ref.ly/Amos4:9) · [MIC 4:4](https://ref.ly/Mic4:4) · [NAM 3:12](https://ref.ly/Nah3:12) · [HAB 3:17](https://ref.ly/Hab3:17) · [HAG 2:19](https://ref.ly/Hag2:19) · [ZEC 3:10](https://ref.ly/Zech3:10)

Sarah Lind

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 3:7; Numbers 13:23; Numbers 20:5; Deuteronomy 8:8; Judges 9:10; Judges 9:11; 1 Kings 5:5; 2 Kings 18:31; 2 Kings 20:7; Nehemiah 13:15; Psalms 105:33; Proverbs 27:18; Song of Songs 2:13; Isaiah 34:4; Isaiah 36:16; Isaiah 38:21; Jeremiah 5:17; Jeremiah 8:13; Jeremiah 24:1; Jeremiah 24:2; Jeremiah 24:3; Jeremiah 24:5; Jeremiah 24:8; Jeremiah 29:17; Hosea 2:14; Hosea 9:10; Joel 1:7; Joel 1:12; Joel 2:22; Amos 4:9; Micah 4:4; Nahum 3:12; Habakkuk 3:17; Haggai 2:19; Zechariah 3:10

## תְּאַשּׁוּר (id: 007702000000000)

תְּאַשּׁוּר
===========

תְּאַשּׁוּר (H8391 · H0839) — תְּאַשּׁוּר

noun f

Trees 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ אֶרֶז · בְּרֹושׁ · הֲדַס · עֵץ שֶׁמֶן · שִׁטָּה · תִּדְהָר

cypress, fir, juniper exact meaning unsure: \= one of the evergreen trees commonly found in the Lebanon, with round leaves rather than flat; its fruit is a a mostly inedible seed\-bearing, fleshy cone; ≈ regarded as one of the glorious trees of the Lebanon

[ISA 41:19](https://ref.ly/Isa41:19) · [ISA 60:13](https://ref.ly/Isa60:13) · [EZK 27:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:6)1

[GEN 47:24](https://ref.ly/Gen47:24) · [EXO 23:10](https://ref.ly/Exod23:10) · [LEV 19:25](https://ref.ly/Lev19:25) · [LEV 23:39](https://ref.ly/Lev23:39) · [LEV 25:3](https://ref.ly/Lev25:3) · [LEV 25:7](https://ref.ly/Lev25:7) · [LEV 25:12](https://ref.ly/Lev25:12) · [LEV 25:15](https://ref.ly/Lev25:15) · [LEV 25:16](https://ref.ly/Lev25:16) · [LEV 25:20](https://ref.ly/Lev25:20) · [LEV 25:21](https://ref.ly/Lev25:21) · [LEV 25:22](https://ref.ly/Lev25:22) · [LEV 25:22](https://ref.ly/Lev25:22) · [NUM 18:30](https://ref.ly/Num18:30) · [NUM 18:30](https://ref.ly/Num18:30) · [DEU 14:22](https://ref.ly/Deut14:22) · [DEU 14:28](https://ref.ly/Deut14:28) · [DEU 16:15](https://ref.ly/Deut16:15) · [DEU 22:9](https://ref.ly/Deut22:9) · [DEU 26:12](https://ref.ly/Deut26:12) · [DEU 33:14](https://ref.ly/Deut33:14) · [JOS 5:12](https://ref.ly/Josh5:12) · [2KI 8:6](https://ref.ly/2Kgs8:6) · [2CH 31:5](https://ref.ly/2Chr31:5) · [2CH 32:28](https://ref.ly/2Chr32:28) · [NEH 9:37](https://ref.ly/Neh9:37) · [JOB 31:12](https://ref.ly/Job31:12) · [PSA 107:37](https://ref.ly/Ps107:37) · [PRO 3:9](https://ref.ly/Prov3:9) · [PRO 14:4](https://ref.ly/Prov14:4) · [PRO 18:20](https://ref.ly/Prov18:20) · [ISA 23:3](https://ref.ly/Isa23:3) · [ISA 30:23](https://ref.ly/Isa30:23) · [JER 2:3](https://ref.ly/Jer2:3)1 · [JER 12:13](https://ref.ly/Jer12:13) · [EZK 48:18](https://ref.ly/Ezek48:18)

Happen 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ פְּרִי

profit, revenue, gain literally: yield, produce; hence: \= the resulting effect of one's acts or decisions

## תָּוֶךְ (id: 007744000000000)

תָּוֶךְ
=======

תָּוֶךְ (H8432)

noun m · תִּיכֹון

Space

middle, between \= the line that divides an object or distance into two more or less equal halves

[GEN 1:6](https://ref.ly/Gen1:6) · [GEN 15:10](https://ref.ly/Gen15:10) · [EXO 14:16](https://ref.ly/Exod14:16) · [EXO 14:22](https://ref.ly/Exod14:22) · [EXO 14:23](https://ref.ly/Exod14:23) · [EXO 14:27](https://ref.ly/Exod14:27) · [EXO 14:29](https://ref.ly/Exod14:29) · [EXO 15:19](https://ref.ly/Exod15:19) · [EXO 26:28](https://ref.ly/Exod26:28) · [EXO 28:33](https://ref.ly/Exod28:33) · [EXO 36:33](https://ref.ly/Exod36:33) · [EXO 39:25](https://ref.ly/Exod39:25) · [EXO 39:25](https://ref.ly/Exod39:25) · [NUM 33:8](https://ref.ly/Num33:8) · [DEU 3:16](https://ref.ly/Deut3:16) · [JOS 8:22](https://ref.ly/Josh8:22) · [JOS 12:2](https://ref.ly/Josh12:2) · [JOS 13:9](https://ref.ly/Josh13:9) · [JOS 13:16](https://ref.ly/Josh13:16) · [JDG 15:4](https://ref.ly/Judg15:4) · [2SA 24:5](https://ref.ly/2Sam24:5) · [NEH 9:11](https://ref.ly/Neh9:11) · [PSA 68:26](https://ref.ly/Ps68:26) · [PSA 136:14](https://ref.ly/Ps136:14) · [JER 39:3](https://ref.ly/Jer39:3) · [EZK 15:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek15:4)

Space

middle, midst, center \= the area in the center of a location

## תֹּועָה (id: 007755000000000)

תֹּועָה
=======

תֹּועָה (H8442)

noun f · תעה

Non\-Know

confusion literally: wandering (in one's mind); hence: \= state in which humans are uncertain about what is happening and what they should do

[NEH 4:2](https://ref.ly/Neh4:2)

Unfaithful

leading astray literally: making to wander; hence: \= causative action by which humans cause other humans to depart from a morally and ethically correct course

[ISA 32:6](https://ref.ly/Isa32:6)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Nehemiah 4:2; Isaiah 32:6


## תֹּועָפֹות (id: 007756000000000)

תֹּועָפֹות
==========

תֹּועָפֹות (H8443)

noun f

High

heights, tops, peaks only found in plural; meaning unsure, probably: \= the pointed top of a mountain

[PSA 95:4](https://ref.ly/Ps95:4)

Good

precious exact meaning unknown; literally: heights; hence, possibly: \= state in which objects are considered valuable and desirable

[JOB 22:25](https://ref.ly/Job22:25)1

Animals

horn literally: height (of animal); hence: \= outgrowth of bone encased in hardened skin, often curved and pointed, found in pairs on the heads of cattle, sheep, goats, and other animals; ► used for defending itself against aggression or for attacking other animals; ≈ associated with strength and honor; a raised horn symbolizes confidence and/or pride

[NUM 23:22](https://ref.ly/Num23:22) · [NUM 24:8](https://ref.ly/Num24:8)

1 JOB 22:25 RSV NJPS NRSV ESV "precious" NIV "choicest" \| NJB "piled in heaps" GNT "piled high" \| REB "in double measure"

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 95:4; Job 22:25; Numbers 23:22; Numbers 24:8

## תֹּור (id: 007760000000000)

תֹּור
=====

תֹּור (H8447 · H8448 · H8449 · H8450)

noun c

Birds

dove, pigeon \= a bird with a blue\-gray color with a pinkish sheen to the neck feathers and a black tip on its tail; lives in large colonies and eats mainly seeds; courts, mates, and has nests several times a year; nests on rock ledges; ◄ \|iColumba livia\|i\*; ► used as food and for sacrifices; ≈ regarded as swift, docile, and innocent, but also as silly and senseless; associated with affection, fertility and sexuality because of its mating habits; the moaning sound this bird sometimes makes is associated with pain and suffering

[GEN 15:9](https://ref.ly/Gen15:9) · [LEV 1:14](https://ref.ly/Lev1:14) · [LEV 5:7](https://ref.ly/Lev5:7) · [LEV 5:11](https://ref.ly/Lev5:11) · [LEV 12:6](https://ref.ly/Lev12:6) · [LEV 12:8](https://ref.ly/Lev12:8) · [LEV 14:22](https://ref.ly/Lev14:22) · [LEV 14:30](https://ref.ly/Lev14:30) · [LEV 15:14](https://ref.ly/Lev15:14) · [LEV 15:29](https://ref.ly/Lev15:29) · [NUM 6:10](https://ref.ly/Num6:10) · [PSA 74:19](https://ref.ly/Ps74:19) · [SNG 2:12](https://ref.ly/Song2:12) · [JER 8:7](https://ref.ly/Jer8:7)

noun m

Happen

turn \= an opportunity or obligation to do something that comes successively to each of a number of people

[EST 2:12](https://ref.ly/Esth2:12) · [EST 2:15](https://ref.ly/Esth2:15)

noun m

Jewellery

earring exact meaning unknown; probably: \= a piece of jewellery worn on the lobe of the ear

[SNG 1:10](https://ref.ly/Song1:10) · [SNG 1:11](https://ref.ly/Song1:11)

noun m

Great

rank, distinction exact meaning unknown; possibly: \= state in which humans have a relatively high status

[1CH 17:17](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:17)1

noun m

Domestic Animals

head of cattle \= large ruminant animal with horns and cloven hoofs, ► domesticated primarily for meat or milk, as a beast of burden, or for pulling a cart or a plow; a clean animal which can be eaten and sacrificed

[EZR 6:9](https://ref.ly/Ezra6:9) · [EZR 6:17](https://ref.ly/Ezra6:17) · [EZR 7:17](https://ref.ly/Ezra7:17) · [DAN 4:22](https://ref.ly/Dan4:22) · [DAN 4:29](https://ref.ly/Dan4:29) · [DAN 4:30](https://ref.ly/Dan4:30) · [DAN 5:21](https://ref.ly/Dan5:21)

תֹּורָה
=======

teaching, instruction \= causative action by which humans in a position of authority and possessing a certain amount of wisdom or skill cause (other) humans to acquire knowledge, a skill, or to emulate a certain type of behavior

 noun f sg

## תֹּושָׁב (id: 007762000000000)

תֹּושָׁב
========

תֹּושָׁב (H8453)

noun m · ישׁב

Classes 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ גֵּר

sojourner \= state in which humans live in a place which is not their place of origin or nationality, either permanently or for a substantial period of time

=========

noun f · זנה

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ זִמָּה · תֹּועֵבָה

promiscuity, debauchery, prostitution, harlotry, whoring, fornication \= action by which humans engage in sexual activity that is considered immoral; ≈ used exclusively as a metaphor for unfaithfulness to God by worshiping idols

======

תֹּחוּ (H8459)

name

Names of People 

|  |
| --- |

noun m

Birds

short\-eared owl exact meaning unknown; possibly: \= type of owl, medium\-sized and with a brown color, but with a paler face and ear tufts that are not very prominent; it makes a strange sound like an animal or a person snoring; it lives in grassland and semi desert regions; ◄ Asio flammeus; ► unclean and therefore not to be eaten

Birds

nightjar, nighthawk exact meaning unknown; possibly: \= speckled brown bird that is about 15 centimeters (6 inches) long, with a short beak that can open very wide; it flies by night and feeds on flying insects; during the day they roost on the ground or on thick branches; their presence in an area is known from their calls at night; ◄ Caprimulgus nubicus or Caprimulgus europaeus; ► unclean and therefore not to be eaten

Associate

among literally: under (a group); hence: \= state in which humans or objects are part of a group of other humans or objects

Control

under the authority (of) literally: under (someone else); hence: \= state in which humans or objects are in a position of subordination to (other) humans, who are sometimes represented metonymically by body parts such as their hand and feet

instead of, in exchange for literally: under (a person or object); hence: \= state in which humans, objects, or events are substituted by other humans, objects, or events

Occurrence

when ... happens, under, amid literally: under (an event); hence: \= state in which an event happens simultaneously with another event

[JOB 30:14](https://ref.ly/Job30:14) · [PRO 30:21](https://ref.ly/Prov30:21) · [PRO 30:21](https://ref.ly/Prov30:21) · [PRO 30:22](https://ref.ly/Prov30:22) · [PRO 30:23](https://ref.ly/Prov30:23) · [HAB 3:7](https://ref.ly/Hab3:7)

Perception

**Collocation:** תַּחַת אֲשֶׁר

because literally: under (an event); hence: \= state in which an event is presented as the motivation, cause, or reason for another event

Perception

**Collocation:** תַּחַת כִּי

because literally: under (an event); hence: \= state in which an event is presented as the motivation, cause, or reason for another event

[DEU 4:37](https://ref.ly/Deut4:37)

name, noun m

Names of Locations

Tahath \= location ◄ in Sinai peninsula, between Makheloth and Terah; ► Israelites encamped there on their way from Egypt to Canaan

[NUM 33:26](https://ref.ly/Num33:26) · [NUM 33:27](https://ref.ly/Num33:27)

Names of People

## תִּירֹושׁ (id: 007796000000000)

תִּירֹושׁ
=========

תִּירֹושׁ (H8492) — תִּירֹשׁ

noun m · ירשׁ

Liquids 

|  |
| --- |

 Wine 

|  |
| --- |

 Crops 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ דְּבַשׁ · דָּגָן · יַיִן · יִצְהָר · פֵּשֶׁת · צֶמֶר

must, (new) wine \= dark red alcoholic liquid; ◄ made out of newly harvested grapes and possibly still at the beginning of the fermentation process; ► used as beverage and for sacrifice; ≈ represents the entire range of agricultural products in Israel, together with grain and oil; associated with joy and well\-being, and only once with drunkenness and foolishness1

## תמם (id: 007853000000000)

תמם
===

תמם (H8552)

verb · תָּם · תֹּם · תֻּמָּה · תָּמִים · תֻּמִּים · יֹותָם

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to be finished, to be spent, to be completed, to be over, to come to an end, to stop \= process by which events reach the stage of completion

תִּנְשֶׁמֶת
===========

תִּנְשֶׁמֶת (H8580)

noun f · נשׁם

Birds

barn owl exact meaning unknown; probably: \= type of owl with a very pale color, light fawn or gray on the wings and back, and almost white on the chest and under the wings; it has small eyes, a large head for its size, and a very striking heart\-shaped white facial disk outlined in brown; it often roosts in barns, deserted houses, caves, and tombs; it lives mainly on rats, mice, and other small nocturnal creatures; ◄ Tyto alba; ► unclean and therefore not to be eaten

[LEV 11:18](https://ref.ly/Lev11:18)1 · [DEU 14:16](https://ref.ly/Deut14:16)1

Small Animals

chameleon \= type of lizard with a basically green color, but which can change color to match its environment; it is slow moving; it feeds on insects by catching them with its long, sticky, elastic tongue, which it flicks at the prey; it is also able to use its tail to wrap around twigs and other things to support itself when the wind blows or when climbing at a steep angle; ◄ Chamaeleo chamaeleon; ► unclean and therefore not to be eaten

[LEV 11:30](https://ref.ly/Lev11:30)2

## תֹּף (id: 007896000000000)

תֹּף
====

תֹּף (H8596)

noun m · תפף

Musical Instruments

drum, hand drum \= musical instrument, consisting of a membrane, usually of animal skin, which was stretched over a shallow circular, triangular, or square frame; ► it was struck sharply with one or two hands, depending on where it was situated; it could be held in one hand, under the arm, or against the chest and struck with the other hand, or it could be held on the knees or the ground and struck with one or two hands; the fingers of one hand could be used to tighten or loosen the tension on the membrane as it was struck

noun m · נפח

Trees 

|  |
| --- |

 Fruits

apple tree, apple \= a tree that reaches a height of 5–10 meters; it has a rounded crown, and bears a round fruit about the size of an orange; in the spring the tree is completely covered with pink flowers, which gradually give way to the green of the leaves as they develop; the fruit can be greenish, yellow, or red. ◄ Malus sylvestris; ► considered both beautiful and refreshing

## תְּרוּעָה (id: 007941000000000)

|  |
| --- |
